ESTOY EN GENERICA ******************* SELECT ta.idarticulo, a.nombre, ta.cantidad ,ta.idarticulo AS id 
                FROM transaccionarticulo ta
                INNER JOIN articulo a ON a.idarticulo = ta.idarticulo
                WHERE ta.idtransaccion=20100019
                AND ta.idestado=1
SELECT ta.idarticulo, a.nombre, ta.cantidad ,ta.idarticulo AS id 
                FROM transaccionarticulo ta
                INNER JOIN articulo a ON a.idarticulo = ta.idarticulo
                WHERE ta.idtransaccion=20100019
                AND ta.idestado=1 ORDER BY idarticulo asc;

ESTOY EN GENERICA ******************* SELECT t.idtransaccion, t.fechainicio, t.fechaactual, e.idestado AS idestado, e.descripcion AS descestado, 
    			s.descripcion AS idseccion, a.descripcion AS idalmacen, '' as edit, '' as view,
    			concat('idtransaccion=',t.idtransaccion) AS id 
                FROM transaccion t
                INNER JOIN seccion a ON a.idseccion = t.idalmacen 
                INNER JOIN seccion s ON s.idseccion = t.idorigen 
                INNER JOIN estadotransaccion e ON e.idestado = t.idestado  WHERE t.idorigen IN (1,2)
SELECT t.idtransaccion, t.fechainicio, t.fechaactual, e.idestado AS idestado, e.descripcion AS descestado, 
    			s.descripcion AS idseccion, a.descripcion AS idalmacen, '' as edit, '' as view,
    			concat('idtransaccion=',t.idtransaccion) AS id 
                FROM transaccion t
                INNER JOIN seccion a ON a.idseccion = t.idalmacen 
                INNER JOIN seccion s ON s.idseccion = t.idorigen 
                INNER JOIN estadotransaccion e ON e.idestado = t.idestado  WHERE t.idorigen IN (1,2) ORDER BY idtransaccion asc;
ESTOY EN GENERICA ******************* SELECT ta.idarticulo,a.nombre, ta.cantidad,ta.cantidad AS aprobar,'SI' AS autoriza, concat('idtransaccion=',ta.idtransaccion,' AND idarticulo=',ta.idarticulo) AS id FROM transaccionarticulo ta INNER JOIN articulo a ON a.idarticulo = ta.idarticulo WHERE ta.idtransaccion = 20100018 AND ta.idestado = 2
SELECT ta.idarticulo,a.nombre, ta.cantidad,ta.cantidad AS aprobar,'SI' AS autoriza, concat('idtransaccion=',ta.idtransaccion,' AND idarticulo=',ta.idarticulo) AS id FROM transaccionarticulo ta INNER JOIN articulo a ON a.idarticulo = ta.idarticulo WHERE ta.idtransaccion = 20100018 AND ta.idestado = 2 ORDER BY 1 asc;

ESTOY EN GENERICA ******************* SELECT t.idtransaccion, t.fechainicio, t.fechaactual, e.idestado AS idestado, e.descripcion AS descestado, 
    			s.descripcion AS idseccion, a.descripcion AS idalmacen, '' as edit, '' as view,
    			concat('idtransaccion=',t.idtransaccion) AS id 
                FROM transaccion t
                INNER JOIN seccion a ON a.idseccion = t.idalmacen 
                INNER JOIN seccion s ON s.idseccion = t.idorigen 
                INNER JOIN estadotransaccion e ON e.idestado = t.idestado  WHERE t.idalmacen IN (32,52,53) AND t.idestado > 1

    			s.descripcion AS idseccion, a.descripcion AS idalmacen, '' as edit, '' as view,
    			concat('idtransaccion=',t.idtransaccion) AS id 
                FROM transaccion t
                INNER JOIN seccion a ON a.idseccion = t.idalmacen 
                INNER JOIN seccion s ON s.idseccion = t.idorigen 
                INNER JOIN estadotransaccion e ON e.idestado = t.idestado  WHERE t.idalmacen IN (32,52,53) AND t.idestado > 1

    			concat('idtransaccion=',t.idtransaccion) AS id 
                FROM transaccion t
                INNER JOIN seccion a ON a.idseccion = t.idalmacen 
                INNER JOIN seccion s ON s.idseccion = t.idorigen 
                INNER JOIN estadotransaccion e ON e.idestado = t.idestado  WHERE t.idorigen IN (1,2) ORDER BY idtransaccion desc;
ESTOY EN GENERICA ******************* SELECT au.idarticulo,a.nombre, au.cantidad,ifnull(en.cantidad,0) AS entregado,au.cantidad - ifnull(en.cantidad,0) AS entregar, concat('idtransaccion=',au.idtransaccion,' AND idarticulo=',au.idarticulo) AS id FROM transaccionarticulo au LEFT JOIN (SELECT idtransaccion, idarticulo, SUM(cantidad) AS cantidad FROM transaccionarticulo WHERE idestado = 5 GROUP BY idarticulo) en ON au.idtransaccion = en.idtransaccion  AND au.idarticulo = en.idarticulo  INNER JOIN articulo a ON a.idarticulo = au.idarticulo WHERE au.idtransaccion = 20100043 AND au.idestado = 3
SELECT au.idarticulo,a.nombre, au.cantidad,ifnull(en.cantidad,0) AS entregado,au.cantidad - ifnull(en.cantidad,0) AS entregar, concat('idtransaccion=',au.idtransaccion,' AND idarticulo=',au.idarticulo) AS id FROM transaccionarticulo au LEFT JOIN (SELECT idtransaccion, idarticulo, SUM(cantidad) AS cantidad FROM transaccionarticulo WHERE idestado = 5 GROUP BY idarticulo) en ON au.idtransaccion = en.idtransaccion  AND au.idarticulo = en.idarticulo  INNER JOIN articulo a ON a.idarticulo = au.idarticulo WHERE au.idtransaccion = 20100043 AND au.idestado = 3 ORDER BY 1 asc;
